 aap jab hotel main khaane khaane jaaen, to ab aapako pani kii bottle kharidne ke liye adhiktam khudara mulya (MRP) se zyada paise chukaane pad sakate hai
 In fact, the Supreme Court has said that if hotels want, they can charge more money than MRP for a bottle of water
 court ne kaha he ki is maamle main hotel or restaraan MRP kii bandhis main nahin bandha hai
 Justice Rohinton Nariman rejected the central government's argument that hotels which charge more than the MRP fixed for a bottle of water can be fined
 centre sarkaar ne aise hotel maalikon ko jail bhejne kii baat bhi kahi thi
 According to a report by Economic Times, the Supreme Court rejected this argument outright
 report kii maane to supreme court ne isko lekar kaha ki ek graahak jab hotel main jaataa he, to vah sirf pani kii bolat kharidne nahin jaataa
 There she also gets many other facilities
 is vajah se use vahaan sarvice bhi milti he
 The central government had said that charging more money from MRP is not only against the interests of the customers, but it can also become a means of tax evasion
 haalanki federation aaf hotel and restarent association ne sarkaar ke is daawey ko sire se khaarij kar diya
 He said that charging more money than MRP for a bottle of water would not threaten the interests of customers nor would it become a means of tax evasion
 association ne kaha ki hotel or restaurant main graahakon ko sarvice bhi di jaati he
 Because of this, the obligation to sell on MRP does not apply here
 association ne kaha ki agar sarkaar ko legal metrology act, 2009 ke tahat karrwai karne kii ijaajat milti he, to yah iske sadasyon ke liye kaaphi nuksaandaayee sabit hoga
 More than 700 people who were protesting against rising unemployment in the US and rising gap between rich and poor were arrested and later released
